25/*
26egrep \
27'^0x([89][0-9A-F]..|A0..|[AB][0-9A-F][4-9].|[AB][0-9A-F]A0|C[0-6][4-9].|C[0-6]A0)' < /cdrom/unix/mappings/eastasia/ksc/ksc5601.txt | perl tab.pl
28
29------tab.pl
30
31 $n=0;
32
33 while (<>) {
34 local($uhc, $ucs4, %rest) = split;
35 local($u)=hex($ucs4);
36 local($k)=hex($uhc);
37 printf ("\n ") if ($n % 8 eq 0);
38 ++$n;
39 printf (" 0x%04x,", $u);
40 }
41 printf ("\n");
42------
43
44*/
45

3038/* Definitions used in the body of the `gconv' function. */
3039#define CHARSET_NAME "UHC//"
3040#define FROM_LOOP from_uhc
3041#define TO_LOOP to_uhc
3042#define DEFINE_INIT 1
3043#define DEFINE_FINI 1
3044#define MIN_NEEDED_FROM 1
3045#define MAX_NEEDED_FROM 2
3046#define MIN_NEEDED_TO 4
3047#define ONE_DIRECTION 0
3048
3049/* First define the conversion function from UHC to UCS4. */
3050#define MIN_NEEDED_INPUT MIN_NEEDED_FROM
3051#define MAX_NEEDED_INPUT MAX_NEEDED_FROM
3052#define MIN_NEEDED_OUTPUT MIN_NEEDED_TO
3053#define LOOPFCT FROM_LOOP
3054#define BODY \
3055 { \
3056 uint32_t ch = (uint32_t) *inptr; \
3057 \
3058/* half-width Korean Currency WON sign \
3059 \
3060 if (ch == 0x5c) \
3061 ch = 0x20a9; \
3062 else if (ch <= 0x7f) \
3063 ch = (uint32_t) ch; \
3064*/ \
3065 if (ch <= 0x7f) \
3066 ++inptr; \
3067 else if (__builtin_expect (ch <= 0x80, 0) \
3068 || __builtin_expect (ch >= 0xfe, 0) \
3069 || __builtin_expect (ch == 0xc9, 0)) \
3070 { \
3071 /* This is illegal. */ \
3072 STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (1); \
3073 } \
3074 else \
3075 { \
3076 /* Two-byte character. First test whether the next byte \
3077 is also available. */ \
3078 uint32_t ch2; \
3079 \
3080 if (__glibc_unlikely (inptr + 1 >= inend)) \
3081 { \
3082 /* The second character is not available. Store \
3083 the intermediate result. */ \
3084 result = __GCONV_INCOMPLETE_INPUT; \
3085 break; \
3086 } \
3087 \
3088 ch2 = inptr[1]; \
3089 \
3090/* \
3091 Additional code points not present in EUC-KR \
3092 \
3093 1st byte 2nd byte \
3094 0x81-0xa0 0x41-0x5a, 0x61-0x7a, 0x81-0xfe total \
3095 (32) (26) + (26) + (126) = 178 5696 \
3096 \
3097 0xa1-0xc5 0x41-0x5a 0x61-0x7a 0x81-0xa0 \
3098 (37) (26) + (26) + (32) = 84 3108 \
3099 \
3100 0xc6 0x41-0x52 \
3101 (1) (18) 18 \
3102 \
3103 8822 \
3104 \
3105 8822(only in UHC) + 2350(both in EUC-KR and UHC) = 11,172 \
3106*/ \
3107 \
3108 if (ch < 0xa1 || ch2 < 0xa1) \
3109 { \
3110 if (__builtin_expect (ch > 0xc6, 0) \
3111 || __builtin_expect (ch2 < 0x41, 0) \
3112 || __builtin_expect (ch2 > 0xfe, 0) \
3113 || (__builtin_expect (ch2 > 0x5a, 0) && ch2 < 0x61) \
3114 || (__builtin_expect (ch2 > 0x7a, 0) && ch2 < 0x81) \
3115 || (__builtin_expect (ch == 0xc6, 0) && ch2 > 0x52)) \
3116 { \
3117 /* This is not legal. */ \
3118 STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (1); \
3119 } \
3120 \
3121 ch = uhc_extra_to_ucs[ch2 - 0x41 \
3122 - (ch2 > 0x80 ? 12 : (ch2 > 0x60 ? 6 : 0)) \
3123 + (ch < 0xa1 \
3124 ? (ch - 0x81) * 178 \
3125 : 5696 + (ch - 0xa1) * 84)]; \
3126 \
3127 if (__glibc_unlikely (ch == 0)) \
3128 { \
3129 /* This is an illegal character. */ \
3130 STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (2); \
3131 } \
3132 \
3133 inptr += 2; \
3134 } \
3135 else \
3136 { \
3137 ch = ksc5601_to_ucs4 (&inptr, 2, 0x80); \
3138 if (__builtin_expect (ch == __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR, 0) \
3139 || __builtin_expect (ch == 0x327e, 0)) \
3140 { \
3141 /* Illegal. */ \
3142 STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (2); \
3143 } \
3144 } \
3145 } \
3146 \
3147 put32 (outptr, ch); \
3148 outptr += 4; \
3149 }
3150#define LOOP_NEED_FLAGS
3151#define ONEBYTE_BODY \
3152 { \
3153 if (c < 0x80) \
3154 return c; \
3155 else \
3156 return WEOF; \
3157 }
3158#include <iconv/loop.c>
3159
3160
3161/* Next, define the other direction. */
3162#define MIN_NEEDED_INPUT MIN_NEEDED_TO
3163#define MIN_NEEDED_OUTPUT MIN_NEEDED_FROM
3164#define MAX_NEEDED_OUTPUT MAX_NEEDED_FROM
3165#define LOOPFCT TO_LOOP
3166#define BODY \
3167 { \
3168 uint32_t ch = get32 (inptr); \
3169 \
3170 if (ch <= 0x7f) \
3171 /* XXX Think about 0x5c ; '\'. */ \
3172 *outptr++ = ch; \
3173 else if (ch >= 0xac00 && ch <= 0xd7a3) \
3174 { \
3175 const char *s = uhc_hangul_from_ucs[ch - 0xac00]; \
3176 \
3177 if (__glibc_unlikely (outptr + 2 > outend)) \
3178 { \
3179 result = __GCONV_FULL_OUTPUT; \
3180 break; \
3181 } \
3182 \
3183 *outptr++ = s[0]; \
3184 *outptr++ = s[1]; \
3185 } \
3186 else if ((ch >= 0x4e00 && ch <= 0x9fa5) || (ch >= 0xf900 && ch <= 0xfa0b))\
3187 { \
3188 size_t written = ucs4_to_ksc5601_hanja (ch, outptr, outend - outptr); \
3189 \
3190 if (__glibc_unlikely (written == 0)) \
3191 { \
3192 result = __GCONV_FULL_OUTPUT; \
3193 break; \
3194 } \
3195 if (__glibc_unlikely (written == __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR)) \
3196 { \
3197 STANDARD_TO_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (4); \
3198 } \
3199 \
3200 *outptr++ |= 0x80; \
3201 *outptr++ |= 0x80; \
3202 } \
3203/* Half-width Korean Currency Won Sign \
3204 else if (ch == 0x20a9) \
3205 idx = 0x5c00; \
3206*/ \
3207 else \
3208 { \
3209 size_t written = ucs4_to_ksc5601_sym (ch, outptr, outend - outptr); \
3210 \
3211 if (__builtin_expect (ch == 0x327e, 0) \
3212 || __builtin_expect (written == __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR, 0)) \
3213 { \
3214 UNICODE_TAG_HANDLER (ch, 4); \
3215 STANDARD_TO_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (4); \
3216 } \
3217 if (__glibc_unlikely (written == 0)) \
3218 { \
3219 result = __GCONV_FULL_OUTPUT; \
3220 break; \
3221 } \
3222 \
3223 *outptr++ |= 0x80; \
3224 *outptr++ |= 0x80; \
3225 } \
3226 \
3227 inptr += 4; \
3228 }
3229#define LOOP_NEED_FLAGS
3230#include <iconv/loop.c>
